<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zub</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ц</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-éc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубец.html>зубе́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zubéc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубец.html>зубца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубец.html>зубцы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубец.html>зубцо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tooth, cog</li>
<li>jag</li>
<li>merlon, battlement (any of the projections between the embrasures of a battlement)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зубной.html>зубно́й</a> (23546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zub</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубной.html>зубно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zubnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tooth; dental</li></ol>

</p>

</p>

***зубчатый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зубча́тый</a> (15055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубец.html>зубе́ц</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zubéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́тый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (ending-stressed) or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубец.html>зубе́ц</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zubéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-атый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-atyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (stem-stressed).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зубча́тый</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зу́бчатый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zubčátyj</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zúbčatyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>toothed, cogged
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зубча́тая</a></b>/<b><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зу́бчатая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́ча</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zubčátaja</b>/<b>zúbčataja</b> peredáča</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tooth gear(ing)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зубча́тая</a></b>/<b><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зу́бчатая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рейка.html>ре́йка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zubčátaja</b>/<b>zúbčataja</b> réjka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rack</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зубча́тое</a></b>/<b><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зу́бчатое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:колесо.html>колесо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zubčátoje</b>/<b>zúbčatoje</b> kolesó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cogwheel; gear wheel; pinion</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>notched, indented</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зубча́тый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zubčátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is normative; <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зубчатый.html>зу́бчатый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zúbčatyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the stress on the first syllable, is colloquial.</li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>зы́б<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***зыбь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зыбь.html>зыбь</a> (26394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:зыбь.html>зыбь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zybĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unsteady place, quagmire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Derivable synchronically as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зы́б(<a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zýb(kij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зыбь.html>зыбь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zybʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зыбь.html>зы́би</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зыбь.html>зы́би</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зыбь.html>зыбе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ripple, swell <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">surface wave in the absence of wind</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wave <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">generally on the sea</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>unstable surface, quagmire</li></ol>

***зять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зять.html>зять</a> (5812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zętь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵenh₁-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зять.html>зять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зять.html>зя́тя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зять.html>зятья́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зять.html>зятьёв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>son-in-law</li>
<li>brother-in-law <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the husband of one’s sister or sister-in-law</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зять.html>зять</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 2c^  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-зять-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***и.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> (1)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Early Cyrillic letter iže, from Greek Η (“eta”).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">i</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The Cyrillic letter <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">I</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">i</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Roman letter</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> I, i</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">English letter</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> E, e</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*i</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ei</i>, an early locative singular determiner, formed from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁e-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁o-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">εἰ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eἰ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">if</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌴𐌹</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ei</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and, so that, be it</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Follows from ablative <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ed</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_6">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">i</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>and
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:груша.html>гру́ша</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vot jábloko <b>i</b> grúša.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Here’s an apple and a pear.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Da <b>i</b> dáže užé ne bolít</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>And</b> it doesn't even hurt anymore.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Da dáže užé <b>i</b> ne bolít</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>And</b> it doesn't even hurt anymore.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>as well as, both ... and ...
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">росси́и <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>нужны́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:армия.html>а́рмия</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:флот.html>фло́т</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Rossíi nužný <b>i</b> ármija, <b>i</b> flót.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Russia needs an army <b>as well as</b> a navy.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>as well
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>i</b> éto znáju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I know that <b>as well</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>even
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бояться.html>бою́сь</a> дана́йцев <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дар.html>дары́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приносящий.html>принося́щих</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bojúsʹ danájcev <b>i</b> darý prinosjáščix</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I fear the Danaans [Greeks], <b>even</b> those bearing gifts.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>нашёл</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обокрасть.html>обокра́сть</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Da on <b>i</b> jejó ne našól — slóvno nas uspéli obokrástʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And he didn't find <b>even</b> that, as if someone had managed to rob us.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ой.html>Ой́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пытаться.html>пыта́лся</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oj, da ja ž dáže <b>i</b> ne pytálsja!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Oh my! I didn't <b>even</b> try to put any effort! (It can be either sacrasm or not) (<a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> means "even" too)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle_2">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">i</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">preceding a verb</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Emphasizes the truth of the following verb. Note that "<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>" is also used, which is usually omitted.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лает</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On tak <b>i</b> délajet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>does</b> do it that way.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná <b>i</b> pošlá tudá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She <b>did</b> go there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>оно́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Onó <b>i</b> jestʹ takóje.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It <i><b>is</b></i> like that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>i</b> jestʹ tot čelovék.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I <i><b>am</b></i> that person.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ибо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ибо.html>и́бо</a> (880)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ибо.html>и́бо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">íbo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> for, because, as, since</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Though described as literary as of the 20th century, particularly since the 21st century colloquial usage also occurs, where it may be used humorously or as slang, "spicing up" the speech; compare also the Ukrainian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">бо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Regardless of these trends, Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ибо.html>и́бо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ibo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> typically remains being prescribed as literary only.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potomú što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>та́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ták kak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***ива.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ива.html>и́ва</a> (8537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьva</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*H₁eyHweh₂</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">yew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Slavic cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:ива.html>и́ва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">íva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">і́ва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">íva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">iwa</i>. More distant cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄᾱ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">ýr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ijf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Eibe</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ива.html>и́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">íva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ива.html>и́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ива.html>и́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ива.html>ив</a></b>)

***иврит.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иврит.html>иври́т</a> (11739)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">עִבְרִית</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ivrít</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иврит.html>иври́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ivrít</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иврит.html>иври́та</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The Hebrew language, <span class="use-with-mention">especially</span> Modern Hebrew, Ivrit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говорю́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иврит.html>иври́те</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja ne govorjú na <b>ivríte</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't speak <b>Hebrew</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Language names that are nouns form their adverbs with the preposition <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (+ prepositional case), rather than with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. For example: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иврит.html>иври́те</a></b></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na <b>ivríte</b></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in <b>Hebrew</b></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:игла.html>игла</a> (5819)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьgъla</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игла.html>игла́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iglá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игла.html>иглы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игла.html>и́глы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игла.html>и́гл</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>needle</li>
<li>thorn, prickle</li>
<li>quill, spine, bristle</li></ol>
